71// User-level names for subtarget features that participate in
72// instruction matching.
73static const char *getSubtargetFeatureName(uint64_t Val) {
74 switch(Val) {
75 case Feature_UseSoftMulDivBit: return "";
76 case Feature_HasV9Bit: return "";
77 case Feature_HasVISBit: return "";
78 case Feature_HasVIS2Bit: return "";
79 case Feature_HasVIS3Bit: return "";
80 case Feature_HasPWRPSRBit: return "";
81 default: return "(unknown)";
82 }
83}
84
85#endif // GET_SUBTARGET_FEATURE_NAME

91static void applyMnemonicAliases(StringRef &Mnemonic, const FeatureBitset &Features, unsigned VariantID) {
92 switch (VariantID) {
93 case 0:
94 switch (Mnemonic.size()) {
95 default: break;
96 case 4: // 7 strings to match.
97 switch (Mnemonic[0]) {
98 default: break;
99 case 'a': // 1 string to match.
100 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+1, "ddc", 3) != 0)
101 break;
102 if (Features.test(Feature_HasV9Bit)) // "addc"
103 Mnemonic = "addx";
104 return;
105 case 'l': // 1 string to match.
106 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+1, "duw", 3) != 0)
107 break;
108 if (Features.test(Feature_HasV9Bit)) // "lduw"
109 Mnemonic = "ld";
110 return;
111 case 's': // 5 strings to match.
112 switch (Mnemonic[1]) {
113 default: break;
114 case 't': // 4 strings to match.
115 switch (Mnemonic[2]) {
116 default: break;
117 case 's': // 2 strings to match.
118 switch (Mnemonic[3]) {
119 default: break;
120 case 'b': // 1 string to match.
121 Mnemonic = "stb"; // "stsb"
122 return;
123 case 'h': // 1 string to match.
124 Mnemonic = "sth"; // "stsh"
125 return;
126 }
127 break;
128 case 'u': // 2 strings to match.
129 switch (Mnemonic[3]) {
130 default: break;
131 case 'b': // 1 string to match.
132 Mnemonic = "stb"; // "stub"
133 return;
134 case 'h': // 1 string to match.
135 Mnemonic = "sth"; // "stuh"
136 return;
137 }
138 break;
139 }
140 break;
141 case 'u': // 1 string to match.
142 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+2, "bc", 2) != 0)
143 break;

145 Mnemonic = "subx";

148 break;

1577
1578void SparcAsmParser::
1579convertToMCInst(unsigned Kind, MCInst &Inst, unsigned Opcode,
1580 const OperandVector &Operands) {
1581 assert(Kind < CVT_NUM_SIGNATURES && "Invalid signature!");
1582 const uint8_t *Converter = ConversionTable[Kind];
1583 unsigned OpIdx;
1584 Inst.setOpcode(Opcode);
1585 for (const uint8_t *p = Converter; *p; p += 2) {
1586 OpIdx = *(p + 1);
1587 switch (*p) {
1588 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid conversion entry!");
1589 case CVT_Reg:
1590 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addRegOperands(Inst, 1);
1591 break;
1592 case CVT_Tied: {
1593 assert(OpIdx < (size_t)(std::end(TiedAsmOperandTable) -
1594 std::begin(TiedAsmOperandTable)) &&
1595 "Tied operand not found");
1596 unsigned TiedResOpnd = TiedAsmOperandTable[OpIdx][0];
1597 if (TiedResOpnd != (uint8_t)-1)
1598 Inst.addOperand(Inst.getOperand(TiedResOpnd));
1599 break;
1600 }
1601 case CVT_95_Reg:
1602 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addRegOperands(Inst, 1);
1603 break;
1604 case CVT_95_addImmOperands:
1605 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addImmOperands(Inst, 1);
1606 break;
1607 case CVT_imm_95_8:
1608 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(8));
1609 break;
1610 case CVT_imm_95_13:
1611 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(13));
1612 break;
1613 case CVT_imm_95_5:
1614 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(5));
1615 break;
1616 case CVT_imm_95_1:
1617 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(1));
1618 break;
1619 case CVT_imm_95_10:
1620 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(10));
1621 break;
1622 case CVT_imm_95_11:
1623 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(11));
1624 break;
1625 case CVT_imm_95_12:
1626 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(12));
1627 break;
1628 case CVT_imm_95_3:
1629 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3));
1630 break;
1631 case CVT_imm_95_2:
1632 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(2));
1633 break;
1634 case CVT_imm_95_4:
1635 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(4));
1636 break;
1637 case CVT_imm_95_0:
1638 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(0));
1639 break;
1640 case CVT_imm_95_9:
1641 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(9));
1642 break;
1643 case CVT_imm_95_6:
1644 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(6));
1645 break;
1646 case CVT_imm_95_14:
1647 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(14));
1648 break;
1649 case CVT_regG0:
1650 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createReg(SP::G0));
1651 break;
1652 case CVT_imm_95_15:
1653 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(15));
1654 break;
1655 case CVT_imm_95_7:
1656 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(7));
1657 break;
1658 case CVT_95_addCallTargetOperands:
1659 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addCallTargetOperands(Inst, 1);
1660 break;
1661 case CVT_regO7:
1662 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createReg(SP::O7));
1663 break;
1664 case CVT_95_addMEMriOperands:
1665 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addMEMriOperands(Inst, 2);
1666 break;
1667 case CVT_95_addMEMrrOperands:
1668 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addMEMrrOperands(Inst, 2);
1669 break;
1670 case CVT_regFCC0:
1671 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createReg(SP::FCC0));
1672 break;
1673 case CVT_95_addMembarTagOperands:
1674 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addMembarTagOperands(Inst, 1);
1675 break;
1676 case CVT_95_addShiftAmtImm5Operands:
1677 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addShiftAmtImm5Operands(Inst, 1);
1678 break;
1679 case CVT_95_addShiftAmtImm6Operands:
1680 static_cast<SparcOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addShiftAmtImm6Operands(Inst, 1);
1681 break;
1682 }
1683 }
1684}
1685
1686void SparcAsmParser::
1687convertToMapAndConstraints(unsigned Kind,
1688 const OperandVector &Operands) {
1689 assert(Kind < CVT_NUM_SIGNATURES && "Invalid signature!");
1690 unsigned NumMCOperands = 0;
1691 const uint8_t *Converter = ConversionTable[Kind];
1692 for (const uint8_t *p = Converter; *p; p += 2) {
1693 switch (*p) {
1694 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid conversion entry!");
1695 case CVT_Reg:
1696 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1697 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("r");
1698 ++NumMCOperands;
1699 break;
1700 case CVT_Tied:
1701 ++NumMCOperands;
1702 break;
1703 case CVT_95_Reg:
1704 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1705 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("r");
1706 NumMCOperands += 1;
1707 break;
1708 case CVT_95_addImmOperands:
1709 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1710 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1711 NumMCOperands += 1;
1712 break;
1713 case CVT_imm_95_8:
1714 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1715 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1716 ++NumMCOperands;
1717 break;
1718 case CVT_imm_95_13:
1719 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1720 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1721 ++NumMCOperands;
1722 break;
1723 case CVT_imm_95_5:
1724 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1725 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1726 ++NumMCOperands;
1727 break;
1728 case CVT_imm_95_1:
1729 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1730 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1731 ++NumMCOperands;
1732 break;
1733 case CVT_imm_95_10:
1734 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1735 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1736 ++NumMCOperands;
1737 break;
1738 case CVT_imm_95_11:
1739 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1740 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1741 ++NumMCOperands;
1742 break;
1743 case CVT_imm_95_12:
1744 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1745 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1746 ++NumMCOperands;
1747 break;
1748 case CVT_imm_95_3:
1749 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1750 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1751 ++NumMCOperands;
1752 break;
1753 case CVT_imm_95_2:
1754 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1755 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1756 ++NumMCOperands;
1757 break;
1758 case CVT_imm_95_4:
1759 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1760 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1761 ++NumMCOperands;
1762 break;
1763 case CVT_imm_95_0:
1764 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1765 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1766 ++NumMCOperands;
1767 break;
1768 case CVT_imm_95_9:
1769 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1770 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1771 ++NumMCOperands;
1772 break;
1773 case CVT_imm_95_6:
1774 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1775 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1776 ++NumMCOperands;
1777 break;
1778 case CVT_imm_95_14:
1779 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1780 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1781 ++NumMCOperands;
1782 break;
1783 case CVT_regG0:
1784 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1785 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1786 ++NumMCOperands;
1787 break;
1788 case CVT_imm_95_15:
1789 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1790 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1791 ++NumMCOperands;
1792 break;
1793 case CVT_imm_95_7:
1794 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1795 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1796 ++NumMCOperands;
1797 break;
1798 case CVT_95_addCallTargetOperands:
1799 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1800 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1801 NumMCOperands += 1;
1802 break;
1803 case CVT_regO7:
1804 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1805 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1806 ++NumMCOperands;
1807 break;
1808 case CVT_95_addMEMriOperands:
1809 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1810 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1811 NumMCOperands += 2;
1812 break;
1813 case CVT_95_addMEMrrOperands:
1814 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1815 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1816 NumMCOperands += 2;
1817 break;
1818 case CVT_regFCC0:
1819 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1820 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1821 ++NumMCOperands;
1822 break;
1823 case CVT_95_addMembarTagOperands:
1824 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1825 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1826 NumMCOperands += 1;
1827 break;
1828 case CVT_95_addShiftAmtImm5Operands:
1829 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1830 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1831 NumMCOperands += 1;
1832 break;
1833 case CVT_95_addShiftAmtImm6Operands:
1834 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1835 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1836 NumMCOperands += 1;
1837 break;
1838 }
1839 }
1840}

1842namespace {
1843
1844/// MatchClassKind - The kinds of classes which participate in
1845/// instruction matching.
1846enum MatchClassKind {
1847 InvalidMatchClass = 0,
1848 OptionalMatchClass = 1,
1849 MCK__PCT_cq, // '%cq'
1850 MCK__PCT_csr, // '%csr'
1851 MCK__PCT_fcc0, // '%fcc0'
1852 MCK__PCT_fq, // '%fq'
1853 MCK__PCT_fsr, // '%fsr'
1854 MCK__PCT_g0, // '%g0'
1855 MCK__PCT_icc, // '%icc'
1856 MCK__PCT_psr, // '%psr'
1857 MCK__PCT_tbr, // '%tbr'
1858 MCK__PCT_wim, // '%wim'
1859 MCK__PCT_xcc, // '%xcc'
1860 MCK__43_, // '+'
1861 MCK_1, // '1'
1862 MCK_10, // '10'
1863 MCK_3, // '3'
1864 MCK_5, // '5'
1865 MCK__91_, // '['
1866 MCK__93_, // ']'
1867 MCK_a, // 'a'
1868 MCK_pn, // 'pn'
1869 MCK_pt, // 'pt'
1870 MCK_LAST_TOKEN = MCK_pt,
1871 MCK_FCCRegs, // register class 'FCCRegs'
1872 MCK_LowQFPRegs, // register class 'LowQFPRegs'
1873 MCK_PRRegs, // register class 'PRRegs'
1874 MCK_CoprocPair, // register class 'CoprocPair'
1875 MCK_IntPair, // register class 'IntPair'
1876 MCK_LowDFPRegs, // register class 'LowDFPRegs'
1877 MCK_QFPRegs, // register class 'QFPRegs'
1878 MCK_ASRRegs, // register class 'ASRRegs'
1879 MCK_CoprocRegs, // register class 'CoprocRegs'
1880 MCK_DFPRegs, // register class 'DFPRegs'
1881 MCK_FPRegs, // register class 'FPRegs'
1882 MCK_IntRegs, // register class 'IntRegs,I64Regs'
1883 MCK_LAST_REGISTER = MCK_IntRegs,
1884 MCK_Imm, // user defined class 'ImmAsmOperand'
1885 MCK_CallTarget, // user defined class 'SparcCallTargetAsmOperand'
1886 MCK_MEMri, // user defined class 'SparcMEMriAsmOperand'
1887 MCK_MEMrr, // user defined class 'SparcMEMrrAsmOperand'
1888 MCK_MembarTag, // user defined class 'SparcMembarTagAsmOperand'
1889 MCK_ShiftAmtImm5, // user defined class 'anonymous_2347'
1890 MCK_ShiftAmtImm6, // user defined class 'anonymous_2348'
1891 NumMatchClassKinds
1892};
1893
1894} // end anonymous namespace
1895
1896static unsigned getDiagKindFromRegisterClass(MatchClassKind RegisterClass) {
1897 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_InvalidOperand;
1898}
1899
1900static MatchClassKind matchTokenString(StringRef Name) {
1901 switch (Name.size()) {
1902 default: break;
1903 case 1: // 7 strings to match.
1904 switch (Name[0]) {
1905 default: break;
1906 case '+': // 1 string to match.
1907 return MCK__43_; // "+"
1908 case '1': // 1 string to match.
1909 return MCK_1; // "1"
1910 case '3': // 1 string to match.
1911 return MCK_3; // "3"
1912 case '5': // 1 string to match.
1913 return MCK_5; // "5"
1914 case '[': // 1 string to match.
1915 return MCK__91_; // "["
1916 case ']': // 1 string to match.
1917 return MCK__93_; // "]"
1918 case 'a': // 1 string to match.
1919 return MCK_a; // "a"
1920 }
1921 break;
1922 case 2: // 3 strings to match.
1923 switch (Name[0]) {
1924 default: break;
1925 case '1': // 1 string to match.
1926 if (Name[1] != '0')
1927 break;
1928 return MCK_10; // "10"
1929 case 'p': // 2 strings to match.
1930 switch (Name[1]) {
1931 default: break;
1932 case 'n': // 1 string to match.
1933 return MCK_pn; // "pn"
1934 case 't': // 1 string to match.
1935 return MCK_pt; // "pt"
1936 }
1937 break;
1938 }
1939 break;
1940 case 3: // 3 strings to match.
1941 if (Name[0] != '%')
1942 break;
1943 switch (Name[1]) {
1944 default: break;
1945 case 'c': // 1 string to match.
1946 if (Name[2] != 'q')
1947 break;
1948 return MCK__PCT_cq; // "%cq"
1949 case 'f': // 1 string to match.
1950 if (Name[2] != 'q')
1951 break;
1952 return MCK__PCT_fq; // "%fq"
1953 case 'g': // 1 string to match.
1954 if (Name[2] != '0')
1955 break;
1956 return MCK__PCT_g0; // "%g0"
1957 }
1958 break;
1959 case 4: // 7 strings to match.
1960 if (Name[0] != '%')
1961 break;
1962 switch (Name[1]) {
1963 default: break;
1964 case 'c': // 1 string to match.
1965 if (memcmp(Name.data()+2, "sr", 2) != 0)
1966 break;
1967 return MCK__PCT_csr; // "%csr"
1968 case 'f': // 1 string to match.
1969 if (memcmp(Name.data()+2, "sr", 2) != 0)
1970 break;
1971 return MCK__PCT_fsr; // "%fsr"
1972 case 'i': // 1 string to match.
1973 if (memcmp(Name.data()+2, "cc", 2) != 0)
1974 break;
1975 return MCK__PCT_icc; // "%icc"
1976 case 'p': // 1 string to match.
1977 if (memcmp(Name.data()+2, "sr", 2) != 0)
1978 break;
1979 return MCK__PCT_psr; // "%psr"
1980 case 't': // 1 string to match.
1981 if (memcmp(Name.data()+2, "br", 2) != 0)
1982 break;
1983 return MCK__PCT_tbr; // "%tbr"
1984 case 'w': // 1 string to match.
1985 if (memcmp(Name.data()+2, "im", 2) != 0)
1986 break;
1987 return MCK__PCT_wim; // "%wim"
1988 case 'x': // 1 string to match.
1989 if (memcmp(Name.data()+2, "cc", 2) != 0)
1990 break;
1991 return MCK__PCT_xcc; // "%xcc"
1992 }
1993 break;
1994 case 5: // 1 string to match.
1995 if (memcmp(Name.data()+0, "%fcc0", 5) != 0)
1996 break;
1997 return MCK__PCT_fcc0; // "%fcc0"
1998 }
1999 return InvalidMatchClass;
2000}
2001
2002/// isSubclass - Compute whether \p A is a subclass of \p B.
2003static bool isSubclass(MatchClassKind A, MatchClassKind B) {
2004 if (A == B)
2005 return true;
2006
2007 switch (A) {
2008 default:
2009 return false;
2010
2011 case MCK_LowQFPRegs:
2012 return B == MCK_QFPRegs;
2013
2014 case MCK_LowDFPRegs:
2015 return B == MCK_DFPRegs;
2016 }
2017}
2018
2019static unsigned validateOperandClass(MCParsedAsmOperand &GOp, MatchClassKind Kind) {
2020 SparcOperand &Operand = (SparcOperand &)GOp;
2021 if (Kind == InvalidMatchClass)
2022 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_InvalidOperand;
2023
2024 if (Operand.isToken() && Kind <= MCK_LAST_TOKEN)
2025 return isSubclass(matchTokenString(Operand.getToken()), Kind) ?
2026 MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success :
2027 MCTargetAsmParser::Match_InvalidOperand;
2028
2029 switch (Kind) {
2030 default: break;
2031 // 'Imm' class
2032 case MCK_Imm: {
2033 DiagnosticPredicate DP(Operand.isImm());
2034 if (DP.isMatch())
2035 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success;
2036 break;
2037 }
2038 // 'CallTarget' class
2039 case MCK_CallTarget: {
2040 DiagnosticPredicate DP(Operand.isCallTarget());
2041 if (DP.isMatch())
2042 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success;
2043 break;
2044 }
2045 // 'MEMri' class
2046 case MCK_MEMri: {
2047 DiagnosticPredicate DP(Operand.isMEMri());
2048 if (DP.isMatch())
2049 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success;
2050 break;
2051 }
2052 // 'MEMrr' class
2053 case MCK_MEMrr: {
2054 DiagnosticPredicate DP(Operand.isMEMrr());
2055 if (DP.isMatch())
2056 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success;
2057 break;
2058 }
2059 // 'MembarTag' class
2060 case MCK_MembarTag: {
2061 DiagnosticPredicate DP(Operand.isMembarTag());
2062 if (DP.isMatch())
2063 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success;
2064 break;
2065 }
2066 // 'ShiftAmtImm5' class
2067 case MCK_ShiftAmtImm5: {
2068 DiagnosticPredicate DP(Operand.isShiftAmtImm5());
2069 if (DP.isMatch())
2070 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success;
2071 break;
2072 }
2073 // 'ShiftAmtImm6' class
2074 case MCK_ShiftAmtImm6: {
2075 DiagnosticPredicate DP(Operand.isShiftAmtImm6());
2076 if (DP.isMatch())
2077 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success;
2078 break;
2079 }
2080 } // end switch (Kind)
2081
2082 if (Operand.isReg()) {
2083 MatchClassKind OpKind;
2084 switch (Operand.getReg()) {
2085 default: OpKind = InvalidMatchClass; break;
2086 case SP::FCC0: OpKind = MCK_FCCRegs; break;
2087 case SP::FCC1: OpKind = MCK_FCCRegs; break;
2088 case SP::FCC2: OpKind = MCK_FCCRegs; break;
2089 case SP::FCC3: OpKind = MCK_FCCRegs; break;
2090 case SP::Y: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2091 case SP::ASR1: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2092 case SP::ASR2: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2093 case SP::ASR3: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2094 case SP::ASR4: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2095 case SP::ASR5: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2096 case SP::ASR6: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2097 case SP::ASR7: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2098 case SP::ASR8: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2099 case SP::ASR9: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2100 case SP::ASR10: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2101 case SP::ASR11: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2102 case SP::ASR12: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2103 case SP::ASR13: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2104 case SP::ASR14: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2105 case SP::ASR15: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2106 case SP::ASR16: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;
2107 case SP::ASR17: OpKind = MCK_ASRRegs; break;

2289 case SP::L0_L1: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2290 case SP::L2_L3: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2291 case SP::L4_L5: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2292 case SP::L6_L7: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2293 case SP::I0_I1: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2294 case SP::I2_I3: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2295 case SP::I4_I5: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2296 case SP::I6_I7: OpKind = MCK_IntPair; break;
2297 case SP::C0_C1: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2298 case SP::C2_C3: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2299 case SP::C4_C5: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2300 case SP::C6_C7: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2301 case SP::C8_C9: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2302 case SP::C10_C11: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2303 case SP::C12_C13: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2304 case SP::C14_C15: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2305 case SP::C16_C17: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2306 case SP::C18_C19: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2307 case SP::C20_C21: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2308 case SP::C22_C23: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2309 case SP::C24_C25: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2310 case SP::C26_C27: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2311 case SP::C28_C29: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2312 case SP::C30_C31: OpKind = MCK_CoprocPair; break;
2313 }
2314 return isSubclass(OpKind, Kind) ? (unsigned)MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success :
2315 getDiagKindFromRegisterClass(Kind);
2316 }
2317
2318 if (Kind > MCK_LAST_TOKEN && Kind <= MCK_LAST_REGISTER)
2319 return getDiagKindFromRegisterClass(Kind);
2320
2321 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_InvalidOperand;
2322}

2375FeatureBitset SparcAsmParser::
2376ComputeAvailableFeatures(const FeatureBitset &FB) const {
2377 FeatureBitset Features;
2378 if (FB[Sparc::FeatureSoftMulDiv])
2379 Features.set(Feature_UseSoftMulDivBit);
2380 if (FB[Sparc::FeatureV9])
2381 Features.set(Feature_HasV9Bit);
2382 if (FB[Sparc::FeatureVIS])
2383 Features.set(Feature_HasVISBit);
2384 if (FB[Sparc::FeatureVIS2])
2385 Features.set(Feature_HasVIS2Bit);
2386 if (FB[Sparc::FeatureVIS3])
2387 Features.set(Feature_HasVIS3Bit);
2388 if (FB[Sparc::FeaturePWRPSR])
2389 Features.set(Feature_HasPWRPSRBit);
2390 return Features;
2391}
2392
2393static bool checkAsmTiedOperandConstraints(const SparcAsmParser&AsmParser,
2394 unsigned Kind,
2395 const OperandVector &Operands,
2396 uint64_t &ErrorInfo) {
2397 assert(Kind < CVT_NUM_SIGNATURES && "Invalid signature!");
2398 const uint8_t *Converter = ConversionTable[Kind];
2399 for (const uint8_t *p = Converter; *p; p += 2) {
2400 switch (*p) {
2401 case CVT_Tied: {
2402 unsigned OpIdx = *(p + 1);
2403 assert(OpIdx < (size_t)(std::end(TiedAsmOperandTable) -
2404 std::begin(TiedAsmOperandTable)) &&
2405 "Tied operand not found");
2406 unsigned OpndNum1 = TiedAsmOperandTable[OpIdx][1];
2407 unsigned OpndNum2 = TiedAsmOperandTable[OpIdx][2];
2408 if (OpndNum1 != OpndNum2) {
2409 auto &SrcOp1 = Operands[OpndNum1];
2410 auto &SrcOp2 = Operands[OpndNum2];
2411 if (SrcOp1->isReg() && SrcOp2->isReg()) {
2412 if (!AsmParser.regsEqual(*SrcOp1, *SrcOp2)) {
2413 ErrorInfo = OpndNum2;
2414 return false;
2415 }
2416 }
2417 }
2418 break;
2419 }
2420 default:
2421 break;
2422 }
2423 }
2424 return true;
2425}

2515namespace {
2516 struct MatchEntry {
2517 uint16_t Mnemonic;
2518 uint16_t Opcode;
2519 uint16_t ConvertFn;
2520 uint8_t RequiredFeaturesIdx;
2521 uint8_t Classes[6];
2522 StringRef getMnemonic() const {
2523 return StringRef(MnemonicTable + Mnemonic + 1,
2524 MnemonicTable[Mnemonic]);
2525 }
2526 };
2527
2528 // Predicate for searching for an opcode.
2529 struct LessOpcode {
2530 bool operator()(const MatchEntry &LHS, StringRef RHS) {
2531 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS;
2532 }
2533 bool operator()(StringRef LHS, const MatchEntry &RHS) {
2534 return LHS < RHS.getMnemonic();
2535 }
2536 bool operator()(const MatchEntry &LHS, const MatchEntry &RHS) {
2537 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS.getMnemonic();
2538 }
2539 };
2540} // end anonymous namespace

4192
4193#include "llvm/Support/Debug.h"
4194#include "llvm/Support/Format.h"
4195
4196unsigned SparcAsmParser::
4197MatchInstructionImpl(const OperandVector &Operands,
4198 MCInst &Inst,
4199 uint64_t &ErrorInfo,
4200 FeatureBitset &MissingFeatures,
4201 bool matchingInlineAsm, unsigned VariantID) {
4202 // Eliminate obvious mismatches.
4203 if (Operands.size() > 7) {
4204 ErrorInfo = 7;
4205 return Match_InvalidOperand;
4206 }
4207
4208 // Get the current feature set.
4209 const FeatureBitset &AvailableFeatures = getAvailableFeatures();
4210
4211 // Get the instruction mnemonic, which is the first token.
4212 StringRef Mnemonic = ((SparcOperand &)*Operands[0]).getToken();
4213
4214 // Process all MnemonicAliases to remap the mnemonic.
4215 applyMnemonicAliases(Mnemonic, AvailableFeatures, VariantID);
4216
4217 // Some state to try to produce better error messages.
4218 bool HadMatchOtherThanFeatures = false;
4219 bool HadMatchOtherThanPredicate = false;
4220 unsigned RetCode = Match_InvalidOperand;
4221 MissingFeatures.set();
4222 // Set ErrorInfo to the operand that mismatches if it is
4223 // wrong for all instances of the instruction.
4224 ErrorInfo = ~0ULL;
4225 // Find the appropriate table for this asm variant.
4226 const MatchEntry *Start, *End;
4227 switch (VariantID) {
4228 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid variant!");
4229 case 0: Start = std::begin(MatchTable0); End = std::end(MatchTable0); break;
4230 }
4231 // Search the table.
4232 auto MnemonicRange = std::equal_range(Start, End, Mnemonic, LessOpcode());
4233
4234 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "AsmMatcher: found " <<
4235 std::distance(MnemonicRange.first, MnemonicRange.second) <<
4236 " encodings with mnemonic '" << Mnemonic << "'\n");
4237
4238 // Return a more specific error code if no mnemonics match.
4239 if (MnemonicRange.first == MnemonicRange.second)
4240 return Match_MnemonicFail;
4241
4242 for (const MatchEntry *it = MnemonicRange.first, *ie = MnemonicRange.second;
4243 it != ie; ++it) {
4244 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures = FeatureBitsets[it->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
4245 bool HasRequiredFeatures =
4246 (AvailableFeatures & RequiredFeatures) == RequiredFeatures;
4247 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "Trying to match opcode "
4248 << MII.getName(it->Opcode) << "\n");
4249 // equal_range guarantees that instruction mnemonic matches.
4250 assert(Mnemonic == it->getMnemonic());
4251 bool OperandsValid = true;
4252 for (unsigned FormalIdx = 0, ActualIdx = 1; FormalIdx != 6; ++FormalIdx) {
4253 auto Formal = static_cast<MatchClassKind>(it->Classes[FormalIdx]);
4254 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4255 dbgs() << " Matching formal operand class " << getMatchClassName(Formal)
4256 << " against actual operand at index " << ActualIdx);
4257 if (ActualIdx < Operands.size())
4258 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << " (";
4259 Operands[ActualIdx]->print(dbgs()); dbgs() << "): ");
4260 else
4261 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << ": ");
4262 if (ActualIdx >= Operands.size()) {
4263 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "actual operand index out of range ");
4264 OperandsValid = (Formal == InvalidMatchClass) || isSubclass(Formal, OptionalMatchClass);
4265 if (!OperandsValid) ErrorInfo = ActualIdx;
4266 break;
4267 }
4268 MCParsedAsmOperand &Actual = *Operands[ActualIdx];
4269 unsigned Diag = validateOperandClass(Actual, Formal);
4270 if (Diag == Match_Success) {
4271 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4272 dbgs() << "match success using generic matcher\n");
4273 ++ActualIdx;
4274 continue;
4275 }
4276 // If the generic handler indicates an invalid operand
4277 // failure, check for a special case.
4278 if (Diag != Match_Success) {
4279 unsigned TargetDiag = validateTargetOperandClass(Actual, Formal);
4280 if (TargetDiag == Match_Success) {
4281 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4282 dbgs() << "match success using target matcher\n");
4283 ++ActualIdx;
4284 continue;
4285 }
4286 // If the target matcher returned a specific error code use
4287 // that, else use the one from the generic matcher.
4288 if (TargetDiag != Match_InvalidOperand && HasRequiredFeatures)
4289 Diag = TargetDiag;
4290 }
4291 // If current formal operand wasn't matched and it is optional
4292 // then try to match next formal operand
4293 if (Diag == Match_InvalidOperand && isSubclass(Formal, OptionalMatchClass)) {
4294 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "ignoring optional operand\n");
4295 continue;
4296 }
4297 // If this operand is broken for all of the instances of this
4298 // mnemonic, keep track of it so we can report loc info.
4299 // If we already had a match that only failed due to a
4300 // target predicate, that diagnostic is preferred.
4301 if (!HadMatchOtherThanPredicate &&
4302 (it == MnemonicRange.first || ErrorInfo <= ActualIdx)) {
4303 if (HasRequiredFeatures && (ErrorInfo != ActualIdx || Diag != Match_InvalidOperand))
4304 RetCode = Diag;
4305 ErrorInfo = ActualIdx;
4306 }
4307 // Otherwise, just reject this instance of the mnemonic.
4308 OperandsValid = false;
4309 break;
4310 }
4311
4312 if (!OperandsValid) {
4313 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "Opcode result: multiple "
4314 "operand mismatches, ignoring "
4315 "this opcode\n");
4316 continue;
4317 }
4318 if (!HasRequiredFeatures) {
4319 HadMatchOtherThanFeatures = true;
4320 FeatureBitset NewMissingFeatures = RequiredFeatures & ~AvailableFeatures;
4321 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "Missing target features:";
4322 for (unsigned I = 0, E = NewMissingFeatures.size(); I != E; ++I)
4323 if (NewMissingFeatures[I])
4324 dbgs() << ' ' << I;
4325 dbgs() << "\n");
4326 if (NewMissingFeatures.count() <=
4327 MissingFeatures.count())
4328 MissingFeatures = NewMissingFeatures;
4329 continue;
4330 }
4331
4332 Inst.clear();
4333
4334 Inst.setOpcode(it->Opcode);
4335 // We have a potential match but have not rendered the operands.
4336 // Check the target predicate to handle any context sensitive
4337 // constraints.
4338 // For example, Ties that are referenced multiple times must be
4339 // checked here to ensure the input is the same for each match
4340 // constraints. If we leave it any later the ties will have been
4341 // canonicalized
4342 unsigned MatchResult;
4343 if ((MatchResult = checkEarlyTargetMatchPredicate(Inst, Operands)) != Match_Success) {
4344 Inst.clear();
4345 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE(
4346 "asm-matcher",
4347 dbgs() << "Early target match predicate failed with diag code "
4348 << MatchResult << "\n");
4349 RetCode = MatchResult;
4350 HadMatchOtherThanPredicate = true;
4351 continue;
4352 }
4353
4354 if (matchingInlineAsm) {
4355 convertToMapAndConstraints(it->ConvertFn, Operands);
4356 if (!checkAsmTiedOperandConstraints(*this, it->ConvertFn, Operands, ErrorInfo))
4357 return Match_InvalidTiedOperand;
4358
4359 return Match_Success;
4360 }
4361
4362 // We have selected a definite instruction, convert the parsed
4363 // operands into the appropriate MCInst.
4364 convertToMCInst(it->ConvertFn, Inst, it->Opcode, Operands);
4365
4366 // We have a potential match. Check the target predicate to
4367 // handle any context sensitive constraints.
4368 if ((MatchResult = checkTargetMatchPredicate(Inst)) != Match_Success) {
4369 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4370 dbgs() << "Target match predicate failed with diag code "
4371 << MatchResult << "\n");
4372 Inst.clear();
4373 RetCode = MatchResult;
4374 HadMatchOtherThanPredicate = true;
4375 continue;
4376 }
4377
4378 if (!checkAsmTiedOperandConstraints(*this, it->ConvertFn, Operands, ErrorInfo))
4379 return Match_InvalidTiedOperand;
4380
4381 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE(
4382 "asm-matcher",
4383 dbgs() << "Opcode result: complete match, selecting this opcode\n");
4384 return Match_Success;
4385 }
4386
4387 // Okay, we had no match. Try to return a useful error code.
4388 if (HadMatchOtherThanPredicate || !HadMatchOtherThanFeatures)
4389 return RetCode;
4390
4391 ErrorInfo = 0;
4392 return Match_MissingFeature;
4393}
4394
4395namespace {
4396 struct OperandMatchEntry {
4397 uint16_t Mnemonic;
4398 uint8_t OperandMask;
4399 uint8_t Class;
4400 uint8_t RequiredFeaturesIdx;
4401
4402 StringRef getMnemonic() const {
4403 return StringRef(MnemonicTable + Mnemonic + 1,
4404 MnemonicTable[Mnemonic]);
4405 }
4406 };
4407
4408 // Predicate for searching for an opcode.
4409 struct LessOpcodeOperand {
4410 bool operator()(const OperandMatchEntry &LHS, StringRef RHS) {
4411 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS;
4412 }
4413 bool operator()(StringRef LHS, const OperandMatchEntry &RHS) {
4414 return LHS < RHS.getMnemonic();
4415 }
4416 bool operator()(const OperandMatchEntry &LHS, const OperandMatchEntry &RHS) {
4417 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS.getMnemonic();
4418 }
4419 };
4420} // end anonymous namespace

4536
4537OperandMatchResultTy SparcAsmParser::
4538tryCustomParseOperand(OperandVector &Operands,
4539 unsigned MCK) {
4540
4541 switch(MCK) {
4542 case MCK_CallTarget:
4543 return parseCallTarget(Operands);
4544 case MCK_MEMri:
4545 return parseMEMOperand(Operands);
4546 case MCK_MEMrr:
4547 return parseMEMOperand(Operands);
4548 case MCK_MembarTag:
4549 return parseMembarTag(Operands);
4550 case MCK_ShiftAmtImm5:
4551 return parseShiftAmtImm<5>(Operands);
4552 case MCK_ShiftAmtImm6:
4553 return parseShiftAmtImm<6>(Operands);
4554 default:
4555 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
4556 }
4557 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
4558}
4559
4560OperandMatchResultTy SparcAsmParser::
4561MatchOperandParserImpl(OperandVector &Operands,
4562 StringRef Mnemonic,
4563 bool ParseForAllFeatures) {
4564 // Get the current feature set.
4565 const FeatureBitset &AvailableFeatures = getAvailableFeatures();
4566
4567 // Get the next operand index.
4568 unsigned NextOpNum = Operands.size() - 1;
4569 // Search the table.
4570 auto MnemonicRange =
4571 std::equal_range(std::begin(OperandMatchTable), std::end(OperandMatchTable),
4572 Mnemonic, LessOpcodeOperand());
4573
4574 if (MnemonicRange.first == MnemonicRange.second)
4575 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
4576
4577 for (const OperandMatchEntry *it = MnemonicRange.first,
4578 *ie = MnemonicRange.second; it != ie; ++it) {
4579 // equal_range guarantees that instruction mnemonic matches.
4580 assert(Mnemonic == it->getMnemonic());
4581
4582 // check if the available features match
4583 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures = FeatureBitsets[it->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
4584 if (!ParseForAllFeatures && (AvailableFeatures & RequiredFeatures) != RequiredFeatures)
4585 continue;
4586
4587 // check if the operand in question has a custom parser.
4588 if (!(it->OperandMask & (1 << NextOpNum)))
4589 continue;
4590
4591 // call custom parse method to handle the operand
4592 OperandMatchResultTy Result = tryCustomParseOperand(Operands, it->Class);
4593 if (Result != MatchOperand_NoMatch)
4594 return Result;
4595 }
4596
4597 // Okay, we had no match.
4598 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
4599}

4601#endif // GET_MATCHER_IMPLEMENTATION

4603
4604#ifdef GET_MNEMONIC_SPELL_CHECKER
4605#undef GET_MNEMONIC_SPELL_CHECKER
4606
4607static std::string SparcMnemonicSpellCheck(StringRef S, const FeatureBitset &FBS, unsigned VariantID) {
4608 const unsigned MaxEditDist = 2;
4609 std::vector<StringRef> Candidates;
4610 StringRef Prev = "";
4611
4612 // Find the appropriate table for this asm variant.
4613 const MatchEntry *Start, *End;
4614 switch (VariantID) {
4615 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid variant!");
4616 case 0: Start = std::begin(MatchTable0); End = std::end(MatchTable0); break;
4617 }
4618
4619 for (auto I = Start; I < End; I++) {
4620 // Ignore unsupported instructions.
4621 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures = FeatureBitsets[I->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
4622 if ((FBS & RequiredFeatures) != RequiredFeatures)
4623 continue;
4624
4625 StringRef T = I->getMnemonic();
4626 // Avoid recomputing the edit distance for the same string.
4627 if (T.equals(Prev))
4628 continue;
4629
4630 Prev = T;
4631 unsigned Dist = S.edit_distance(T, false, MaxEditDist);
4632 if (Dist <= MaxEditDist)
4633 Candidates.push_back(T);
4634 }
4635
4636 if (Candidates.empty())
4637 return "";
4638
4639 std::string Res = ", did you mean: ";
4640 unsigned i = 0;
4641 for (; i < Candidates.size() - 1; i++)
4642 Res += Candidates[i].str() + ", ";
4643 return Res + Candidates[i].str() + "?";
4644}
4645
4646#endif // GET_MNEMONIC_SPELL_CHECKER
4647
4648
4649#ifdef GET_MNEMONIC_CHECKER
4650#undef GET_MNEMONIC_CHECKER
4651
4652static bool SparcCheckMnemonic(StringRef Mnemonic,
4653 const FeatureBitset &AvailableFeatures,
4654 unsigned VariantID) {
4655 // Process all MnemonicAliases to remap the mnemonic.
4656 applyMnemonicAliases(Mnemonic, AvailableFeatures, VariantID);
4657
4658 // Find the appropriate table for this asm variant.
4659 const MatchEntry *Start, *End;
4660 switch (VariantID) {
4661 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid variant!");
4662 case 0: Start = std::begin(MatchTable0); End = std::end(MatchTable0); break;
4663 }
4664
4665 // Search the table.
4666 auto MnemonicRange = std::equal_range(Start, End, Mnemonic, LessOpcode());
4667
4668 if (MnemonicRange.first == MnemonicRange.second)
4669 return false;
4670
4671 for (const MatchEntry *it = MnemonicRange.first, *ie = MnemonicRange.second;
4672 it != ie; ++it) {
4673 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures =
4674 FeatureBitsets[it->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
4675 if ((AvailableFeatures & RequiredFeatures) == RequiredFeatures)
4676 return true;
4677 }
4678 return false;
4679}

4681#endif // GET_MNEMONIC_CHECKER
